<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="M">M</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Jos%C3%A9&amp;action=edit&amp;section=22" title="Edit section: M">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<div class="div-col columns column-width" style="-moz-column-width: 22em; -webkit-column-width: 22em; column-width: 22em;">
<ul><li><a href="/wiki/Jos%C3%A9_Ulises_Mac%C3%ADas_Salcedo" title="José Ulises Macías Salcedo">José Ulises Macías Salcedo</a>, Mexican <a href="/wiki/Bishop_in_the_Catholic_Church" title="Bishop in the Catholic Church">Catholic bishop</a>, Bishop of <a href="/wiki/Roman_Catholic_Diocese_of_Mexicali" title="Roman Catholic Diocese of Mexicali">Mexicali</a>, then <a href="/wiki/Archbishop" title="Archbishop">Archbishop</a> of <a href="/wiki/Roman_Catholic_Archdiocese_of_Hermosillo" title="Roman Catholic Archdiocese of Hermosillo">Hermosillo</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Jos%C3%A9_Malcampo,_3rd_Marquis_of_San_Rafael" class="mw-redirect" title="José Malcampo, 3rd Marquis of San Rafael">José Malcampo y Monge</a>, Spanish <a href="/wiki/Nobility" title="Nobility">noble</a> under the title 3rd Marquis of San Rafael, <a href="/wiki/Admiral" title="Admiral">admiral</a> and <a href="/wiki/Politician" title="Politician">politician</a>, served as <a href="/wiki/List_of_Prime_Ministers_of_Spain" class="mw-redirect" title="List of Prime Ministers of Spain">Prime Minister</a> under <a href="/wiki/Amadeo_I_of_Spain" title="Amadeo I of Spain">King Amadeo I</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Jos%C3%A9_de_Jes%C3%BAs_Madera_Uribe" title="José de Jesús Madera Uribe">José de Jesús Madera Uribe</a>, American member of the <a href="/wiki/Missionaries_of_the_Holy_Spirit" title="Missionaries of the Holy Spirit">Missionaries of the Holy Spirit</a> (M.Sp.S.) and <a href="/wiki/Bishop_in_the_Catholic_Church" title="Bishop in the Catholic Church">Catholic bishop</a>, <a href="/wiki/Coadjutor_bishop" title="Coadjutor bishop">Coadjutor Bishop</a> then Bishop of <a href="/wiki/Roman_Catholic_Diocese_of_Fresno" title="Roman Catholic Diocese of Fresno">Fresno</a>, then <a href="/wiki/Auxiliary_bishop" title="Auxiliary bishop">Auxiliary Bishop</a> to the <a href="/wiki/Roman_Catholic_Archdiocese_for_the_Military_Services,_USA" title="Roman Catholic Archdiocese for the Military Services, USA">Archdiocese for the Military Services, USA</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Jos%C3%A9_Malhoa" title="José Malhoa">José Vital Branco Malhoa</a>, known generally as José Malhoa, Portuguese <a href="/wiki/Painting" title="Painting">painter</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Jos%C3%A9_Manuel_da_C%C3%A2mara_de_Atalaia" title="José Manuel da Câmara de Atalaia">José Manuel da Câmara de Atalaia</a>, Portuguese <a href="/wiki/Politician" title="Politician">statesman</a>, <a href="/wiki/Bishop_in_the_Catholic_Church" title="Bishop in the Catholic Church">Catholic bishop</a> and <a href="/wiki/Cardinal_(Catholic_Church)" title="Cardinal (Catholic Church)">cardinal</a>, before episcopacy appointed to a number of positions by <a href="/wiki/John_V_of_Portugal" title="John V of Portugal">King John V</a> including judge of the Supreme Court of the <a href="/wiki/Portuguese_Inquisition" title="Portuguese Inquisition">Inquisition of Lisbon</a>, and Deputy for the Board of the Three States, then by the king's direction to <a href="/wiki/Pope_Benedict_XIV" title="Pope Benedict XIV">Pope Benedict XIV</a> made Cardinal in 1750, elected as <a href="/wiki/Patriarchate_of_Lisbon" title="Patriarchate of Lisbon">Patriarch of Lisbon</a> in 1754 under the title Dom José I</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Jos%C3%A9_de_la_Mar" title="José de la Mar">José de la Mar</a>, Peruvian military leader to the rank of <a href="/wiki/Brigadier" title="Brigadier">Brigadier</a> and <a href="/wiki/Politician" title="Politician">politician</a>, 2nd and 4th <a href="/wiki/President_of_Peru" title="President of Peru">President of Peru</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Jos%C3%A9_Carlos_Mari%C3%A1tegui" title="José Carlos Mariátegui">José Carlos Mariátegui</a>, Peruvian <a href="/wiki/Intellectual" title="Intellectual">intellectual</a>, <a href="/wiki/Journalist" title="Journalist">journalist</a>, <a href="/wiki/Political_philosophy" title="Political philosophy">political philosopher</a>, and <a href="/wiki/Revolution" title="Revolution">activist</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Jos%C3%A9_Mar%C3%ADn_(composer)" title="José Marín (composer)">José Marin</a>, Spanish <a href="/wiki/Baroque_music" title="Baroque music">Baroque</a> <a href="/wiki/Harpist" class="mw-redirect" title="Harpist">harpist</a>, <a href="/wiki/Guitarist" title="Guitarist">guitarist</a> and <a href="/wiki/Composer" title="Composer">composer</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Jos%C3%A9_Rom%C3%A3o_Martenetz" title="José Romão Martenetz">José Romão Martenetz</a>, Ukrainian-born <a href="/wiki/Monk" title="Monk">monk</a> of the <a href="/wiki/Order_of_Saint_Basil_the_Great" title="Order of Saint Basil the Great">Order of Saint Basil the Great</a> (O.S.B.M.) and Brazilian <a href="/wiki/Ukrainian_Greek_Catholic_Church" title="Ukrainian Greek Catholic Church">Ukrainian Greek Catholic</a> <a href="/wiki/Bishop_in_the_Catholic_Church" title="Bishop in the Catholic Church">bishop</a>, <a href="/wiki/Assistant_bishop" title="Assistant bishop">Assistant Bishop</a> of <a href="/wiki/Roman_Catholic_Archdiocese_of_S%C3%A3o_Sebasti%C3%A3o_do_Rio_de_Janeiro" title="Roman Catholic Archdiocese of São Sebastião do Rio de Janeiro">Rio de Janeiro</a>, <a href="/wiki/Ukrainian_Catholic_Archeparchy_of_S%C3%A3o_Jo%C3%A3o_Batista_em_Curitiba" title="Ukrainian Catholic Archeparchy of São João Batista em Curitiba">Apostolic Exarch (Archbishop) of Brazil</a>, first Eparch (Bishop) of the newly created <a href="/wiki/Ukrainian_Catholic_Eparchy_of_S%C3%A3o_Jo%C3%A3o_Batista_em_Curitiba" class="mw-redirect" title="Ukrainian Catholic Eparchy of São João Batista em Curitiba">Eparchy of São João Batista em Curitiba</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Jos%C3%A9_Mart%C3%AD" title="José Martí">José Julián Martí Pérez</a>, Cuban <a href="/wiki/Poet" title="Poet">poet</a>, <a href="/wiki/Essay" title="Essay">essayist</a>, <a href="/wiki/Journalist" title="Journalist">journalist</a>, <a href="/wiki/Translation" title="Translation">translator</a>, <a href="/wiki/Professor" title="Professor">professor</a>, <a href="/wiki/Publishing" title="Publishing">publisher</a> and <a href="/wiki/Folk_hero" title="Folk hero">national hero</a>, recognised as an important <a href="/wiki/Revolution" title="Revolution">revolutionary</a> <a href="/wiki/Philosopher" title="Philosopher">philosopher</a>, <a href="/wiki/Political_philosophy" title="Political philosophy">political theorist</a> and contributor to <a href="/wiki/Latin_American_literature" title="Latin American literature">Latin American literature</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Jos%C3%A9_Mart%C3%AD_y_Mons%C3%B3" title="José Martí y Monsó">José Martí y Monsó</a>, Spanish <a href="/wiki/Painting" title="Painting">painter</a>, art <a href="/wiki/Professor" title="Professor">professor</a>, <a href="/wiki/Research" title="Research">researcher</a> and <a href="/wiki/Art_museum" title="Art museum">museum</a> official, recognised as an expert on <a href="/wiki/Castile_(historical_region)" title="Castile (historical region)">Castilian</a> art</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Jos%C3%A9_Luis_Mart%C3%AD" title="José Luis Martí">José Luis Martí Soler</a>, retired Spanish professional <a href="/wiki/Association_football" title="Association football">football</a> player and manager</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Jos%C3%A9_Mar%C3%ADa_Mart%C3%ADn_de_Herrera_y_de_la_Iglesia" title="José María Martín de Herrera y de la Iglesia">José María Martín de Herrera y de la Iglesia</a>, Spanish-born <a href="/wiki/Bishop_in_the_Catholic_Church" title="Bishop in the Catholic Church">Catholic bishop</a> and <a href="/wiki/Cardinal_(Catholic_Church)" title="Cardinal (Catholic Church)">cardinal</a> who also served in <a href="/wiki/Cuba" title="Cuba">Cuba</a>, <a href="/wiki/Archbishop" title="Archbishop">Archbishop</a> of <a href="/wiki/Roman_Catholic_Archdiocese_of_Santiago_de_Cuba" title="Roman Catholic Archdiocese of Santiago de Cuba">Santiago de Cuba</a>, then Archbishop of <a href="/wiki/Roman_Catholic_Archdiocese_of_Santiago_de_Compostela" title="Roman Catholic Archdiocese of Santiago de Compostela">Santiago de Compostela</a>, made Cardinal by <a href="/wiki/Pope_Leo_XIII" title="Pope Leo XIII">Pope Leo XIII</a> in 1897</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Jos%C3%A9_Antonio_Mart%C3%ADnez_de_Aldunate" title="José Antonio Martínez de Aldunate">José Antonio Martínez de Aldunate y Garcés de Marcilla</a>, Chilean <a href="/wiki/Bishop_in_the_Catholic_Church" title="Bishop in the Catholic Church">Catholic bishop</a>,  Bishop of Huamanga (now known as the <a href="/wiki/Roman_Catholic_Archdiocese_of_Ayacucho" title="Roman Catholic Archdiocese of Ayacucho">Archdiocese of Ayacucho</a>), Bishop of <a href="/wiki/Roman_Catholic_Archdiocese_of_Santiago_de_Chile" title="Roman Catholic Archdiocese of Santiago de Chile">Santiago de Chile</a>, then Vice President of the 1810 <a href="/wiki/Government_Junta_of_Chile_(1810)" title="Government Junta of Chile (1810)">Junta of Chile</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Jos%C3%A9_Mattoso" title="José Mattoso">José João da Conceição Gonçalves Mattoso</a>, Portuguese <a href="/wiki/Middle_ages" class="mw-redirect" title="Middle ages">Mediaevalist</a> <a href="/wiki/Historian" title="Historian">historian</a> and <a href="/wiki/Professor" title="Professor">professor</a></li>
<li><a href="/w/index.php?title=Jos%C3%A9_Matsuwa&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="José Matsuwa (page does not exist)">José Matsuwa</a>, Mexican <a href="/wiki/Huichol" title="Huichol">Huichol Indian</a> <a href="/wiki/Shamanism" title="Shamanism">shaman</a><sup id="cite_ref-12" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-12">&#91;12&#93;</a></sup></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Jos%C3%A9_Clemente_Maurer" title="José Clemente Maurer">José Clemente Maurer</a>, German-born Bolivian <a href="/wiki/Bishop_in_the_Catholic_Church" title="Bishop in the Catholic Church">Catholic bishop</a> and <a href="/wiki/Cardinal_(Roman_Catholic)" class="mw-redirect" title="Cardinal (Roman Catholic)">cardinal</a>, member of the <a href="/wiki/Congregation_of_the_Most_Holy_Redeemer" title="Congregation of the Most Holy Redeemer">Congregation of the Most Holy Redeemer</a> or Redemptorists (C.Ss.R.), Assistant Bishop of La Paz (now known as the <a href="/wiki/Roman_Catholic_Archdiocese_of_La_Paz" title="Roman Catholic Archdiocese of La Paz">Archdiocese of La Paz</a>), then <a href="/wiki/Archbishop" title="Archbishop">Archbishop</a> of <a href="/wiki/Roman_Catholic_Archdiocese_of_Sucre" title="Roman Catholic Archdiocese of Sucre">Sucre</a>, made Cardinal by <a href="/wiki/Pope_Paul_VI" title="Pope Paul VI">Pope Paul VI</a> in 1967, the first Bolivian to be so appointed</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Jos%C3%A9_Mauri" title="José Mauri">José Agustín Mauri</a>, Argentine-born Italian professional <a href="/wiki/Association_football" title="Association football">football</a> player</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Juan_Jos%C3%A9_Medina" title="Juan José Medina">Juan José Medina</a>,  President of the <a href="/wiki/List_of_Presidents_of_Paraguay" class="mw-redirect" title="List of Presidents of Paraguay">Provisional Junta of Paraguay</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Jos%C3%A9_Carlos_Melo" title="José Carlos Melo">José Carlos Melo</a>, Brazilian <a href="/wiki/Bishop_in_the_Catholic_Church" title="Bishop in the Catholic Church">Catholic bishop</a>, first as <a href="/wiki/Auxiliary_bishop" title="Auxiliary bishop">AuxiliaryBishop</a> of <a href="/wiki/Roman_Catholic_Archdiocese_of_S%C3%A3o_Salvador_da_Bahia" title="Roman Catholic Archdiocese of São Salvador da Bahia">São Salvador da Bahia</a>, then as <a href="/wiki/Archbishop" title="Archbishop">Archbishop</a> of <a href="/wiki/Roman_Catholic_Archdiocese_of_Macei%C3%B3" title="Roman Catholic Archdiocese of Maceió">Maceió</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Jos%C3%A9_Mendes_(athlete)" title="José Mendes (athlete)">José Mendes</a>, Portuguese <a href="/wiki/Sport_of_athletics" title="Sport of athletics">sprinter</a>, <a href="/wiki/Olympic_Games" title="Olympic Games">Olympics</a> competitor</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Jos%C3%A9_Fernando_Ferreira_Mendes" class="mw-redirect" title="José Fernando Ferreira Mendes">José Fernando Ferreira Mendes</a>, often referred to as José F.F. Mendes, Portuguese <a href="/wiki/Physicist" title="Physicist">physicist</a> (<a href="/wiki/Statistical_physics" title="Statistical physics">statistical physics</a>) and <a href="/wiki/Professor" title="Professor">professor</a> of physics, best known for his work in the field of <a href="/wiki/Network_theory" title="Network theory">network theory</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Jos%C3%A9_Mendes_(cyclist)" title="José Mendes (cyclist)">José João Pimenta Costa Mendes</a>, Portuguese <a href="/wiki/Road_bicycle_racing" title="Road bicycle racing">cyclist</a> and international competitor</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Jos%C3%A9_Francisco_Miguel_Ant%C3%B3nio_de_Mendon%C3%A7a" title="José Francisco Miguel António de Mendonça">José Francisco Miguel António de Mendonça</a> or Mendoça, Portuguese <a href="/wiki/Bishop_in_the_Catholic_Church" title="Bishop in the Catholic Church">Catholic bishop</a> and <a href="/wiki/Cardinal_(Catholic_Church)" title="Cardinal (Catholic Church)">cardinal</a>, rector of the <a href="/wiki/University_of_Coimbra" title="University of Coimbra">University of Coimbra</a>, nominated by <a href="/wiki/Peter_III_of_Portugal" title="Peter III of Portugal">King Peter III</a> as <a href="/wiki/Patriarchate_of_Lisbon" title="Patriarchate of Lisbon">Patriarch of Lisbon</a> in 1786 with the name Dom José II, made Cardinal by <a href="/wiki/Pope_Pius_XI" title="Pope Pius XI">Pope Pius XI</a> in 1788</li>
<li><a href="/w/index.php?title=Jos%C3%A9_Mar%C3%ADa_Mercado_de_Luna&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="José María Mercado de Luna (page does not exist)">José María Mercado de Luna</a>, Mexican <a href="/wiki/Priesthood_in_the_Catholic_Church" title="Priesthood in the Catholic Church">Catholic priest</a> and participant in the <a href="/wiki/Mexican_War_of_Independence" title="Mexican War of Independence">Mexican War of Independence</a><sup id="cite_ref-13" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-13">&#91;13&#93;</a></sup></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Jos%C3%A9_Miller" title="José Miller">José Miller</a>, also known as Dr Josie Miller, leader of Cuba's Jewish community and their spokesman with the <a href="/wiki/Politics_of_Cuba" title="Politics of Cuba">Cuban Government</a> under <a href="/wiki/Fidel_Castro" title="Fidel Castro">Fidel Castro</a>'s presidency</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Jos%C3%A9_Adolfo_Mojica_Morales" title="José Adolfo Mojica Morales">José Adolfo Mojica Morales</a>, San Salvadorian <a href="/wiki/Bishop_in_the_Catholic_Church" title="Bishop in the Catholic Church">Catholic bishop</a>, Bishop of <a href="/wiki/Roman_Catholic_Diocese_of_Sonsonate" title="Roman Catholic Diocese of Sonsonate">Sonsonate</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Jos%C3%A9_Rafael_Molina_Ure%C3%B1a" title="José Rafael Molina Ureña">José Rafael Molina Ureña</a>, Dominican <a href="/wiki/Politician" title="Politician">politician</a> and <a href="/wiki/Diplomat" title="Diplomat">diplomat</a>, served briefly as Provisional <a href="/wiki/List_of_Presidents_of_the_Dominican_Republic" class="mw-redirect" title="List of Presidents of the Dominican Republic">President</a> after the <a href="/wiki/Dominican_Civil_War" title="Dominican Civil War">Dominican Civil War</a>, then terms as <a href="/wiki/Permanent_Representative" class="mw-redirect" title="Permanent Representative">Permanent Representative</a> to the <a href="/wiki/United_Nations" title="United Nations">United Nations</a> and Ambassador to France</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Jos%C3%A9_Luis_Mollaghan" title="José Luis Mollaghan">José Luis Mollaghan</a>, Argentinian <a href="/wiki/Bishop_in_the_Catholic_Church" title="Bishop in the Catholic Church">Catholic bishop</a>, <a href="/wiki/Auxiliary_bishop" title="Auxiliary bishop">Auxiliary Bishop</a> of <a href="/wiki/Roman_Catholic_Archdiocese_of_Buenos_Aires" title="Roman Catholic Archdiocese of Buenos Aires">Buenos Aires</a>, Bishop of <a href="/wiki/Roman_Catholic_Diocese_of_San_Miguel_(Argentina)" title="Roman Catholic Diocese of San Miguel (Argentina)">San Miguel</a>, then <a href="/wiki/Archbishop" title="Archbishop">Archbishop</a> of <a href="/wiki/Roman_Catholic_Archdiocese_of_Rosario" title="Roman Catholic Archdiocese of Rosario">Rosario</a>, assigned by <a href="/wiki/Pope_Francis" title="Pope Francis">Pope Francis</a> to the <a href="/wiki/Congregation_for_the_Doctrine_of_the_Faith" title="Congregation for the Doctrine of the Faith">Congregation for the Doctrine of the Faith</a> to work on the handling of clerical <a href="/wiki/Pedophilia" title="Pedophilia">pedophilia</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Jos%C3%A9_Gregorio_Monagas" title="José Gregorio Monagas">José Gregorio Monagas</a>, Venezuelan <a href="/wiki/General_officer" title="General officer">general</a> and <a href="/wiki/Politician" title="Politician">politician</a>, <a href="/wiki/List_of_Presidents_of_Venezuela" class="mw-redirect" title="List of Presidents of Venezuela">President of Venezuela</a>, brother of <a href="/wiki/Jos%C3%A9_Tadeo_Monagas" title="José Tadeo Monagas">José Tadeo Monagas</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Jos%C3%A9_Ruperto_Monagas" title="José Ruperto Monagas">José Ruperto Monagas</a>, <a href="/wiki/List_of_Presidents_of_Venezuela" class="mw-redirect" title="List of Presidents of Venezuela">President of Venezuela</a>, son of <a href="/wiki/Jos%C3%A9_Tadeo_Monagas" title="José Tadeo Monagas">José Tadeo Monagas</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Jos%C3%A9_Tadeo_Monagas" title="José Tadeo Monagas">José Tadeo Monagas Burgos</a>, hero of the <a href="/wiki/Venezuelan_War_of_Independence" title="Venezuelan War of Independence">Venezuelan War of Independence</a>, twice <a href="/wiki/List_of_Presidents_of_Venezuela" class="mw-redirect" title="List of Presidents of Venezuela">President of Venezuela</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Jos%C3%A9_Mar%C3%ADa_Moncada" title="José María Moncada">osé María Moncada Tapia</a>, Nicaraguan <a href="/wiki/Revolution" title="Revolution">revolutionary</a> and <a href="/wiki/Politician" title="Politician">politician</a>, 19th <a href="/wiki/President_of_Nicaragua" title="President of Nicaragua">President of Nicaragua</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Jos%C3%A9_Pablo_Moncayo" title="José Pablo Moncayo">José Pablo Moncayo García</a>, Mexican <a href="/wiki/Pianist" title="Pianist">pianist</a>, <a href="/wiki/Percussion_instrument" title="Percussion instrument">percussionist</a>, <a href="/wiki/Music_education" title="Music education">music teacher</a>, <a href="/wiki/Composer" title="Composer">composer</a> and <a href="/wiki/Conducting" title="Conducting">conductor</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Jos%C3%A9_Mo%C3%B1ino,_1st_Count_of_Floridablanca" title="José Moñino, 1st Count of Floridablanca">José Moñino y Redondo</a>, Spanish <a href="/wiki/Nobility" title="Nobility">noble</a> titled 1st Count of Floridablanca, <a href="/wiki/Jurist" title="Jurist">jurist</a>, <a href="/wiki/Reformism" title="Reformism">reformist</a>, <a href="/wiki/Politician" title="Politician">statesman</a>, served as <a href="/wiki/List_of_Prime_Ministers_of_Spain" class="mw-redirect" title="List of Prime Ministers of Spain">First Secretary of State</a> under Kings <a href="/wiki/Charles_III_of_Spain" title="Charles III of Spain">Charles III</a> and <a href="/wiki/Charles_IV_of_Spain" title="Charles IV of Spain">Charles IV</a>, usually referred to in modern Spain as <i>Conde de Floridablanca</i>, the plant genus <a href="/wiki/Monnina" title="Monnina">Monnina</a> was named after him</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Jos%C3%A9_Pedro_Montero" title="José Pedro Montero">José Pedro Montero De Candia</a>, Paraguayan <a href="/wiki/Pediatrics" title="Pediatrics">paediatrician</a>, university <a href="/wiki/Professor" title="Professor">professor</a> and <a href="/wiki/Politician" title="Politician">politician</a>, 27th <a href="/wiki/List_of_Presidents_of_Paraguay" class="mw-redirect" title="List of Presidents of Paraguay">President of Paraguay</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Jos%C3%A9_Mar%C3%ADa_Montes" title="José María Montes">José María Montes</a>, Argentinian Catholic bishop, <a href="/wiki/Auxiliary_bishop" title="Auxiliary bishop">Auxiliary Archbishop</a> of <a href="/wiki/Roman_Catholic_Archdiocese_of_La_Plata_in_Argentina" title="Roman Catholic Archdiocese of La Plata in Argentina">La Plata</a>, Bishop of <a href="/wiki/Roman_Catholic_Diocese_of_Chascom%C3%BAs" title="Roman Catholic Diocese of Chascomús">Chascomús</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Jos%C3%A9_Mar%C3%ADa_Morelos" title="José María Morelos">José María Teclo Morelos Pérez y Pavón</a>, Mexican <a href="/wiki/Priesthood_in_the_Catholic_Church" title="Priesthood in the Catholic Church">Catholic priest</a> and <a href="/wiki/Revolution" title="Revolution">rebel leader</a> in the <a href="/wiki/Mexican_War_of_Independence" title="Mexican War of Independence">Mexican War of Independence</a>, defrocked and executed for treason</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Jos%C3%A9_Vianna_da_Motta" title="José Vianna da Motta">José Vianna da Motta</a> (sometimes spelt Viana da Mota), Portuguese <a href="/wiki/Pianist" title="Pianist">pianist</a>, <a href="/wiki/Music_education" title="Music education">teacher</a> and <a href="/wiki/Composer" title="Composer">composer</a>, last pupil of <a href="/wiki/Franz_Liszt" title="Franz Liszt">Franz Liszt</a>, the <a href="/wiki/Vianna_da_Motta_International_Music_Competition" title="Vianna da Motta International Music Competition">Vianna da Motta International Music Competition</a> was founded in 1957 in his honour</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Jos%C3%A9_Mourinho" title="José Mourinho">José Mourinho</a>, Portuguese professional <a href="/wiki/Association_football" title="Association football">football</a> coach and former football player</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Jos%C3%A9_Moya" title="José Moya">José David Moya Rojas</a>, Columbian professional <a href="/wiki/Association_football" title="Association football">football</a> player</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Jos%C3%A9_Mujica" title="José Mujica">José Mujica</a>, Venezuelan professional <a href="/wiki/Baseball" title="Baseball">baseball</a> player</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Jos%C3%A9_Mujica" title="José Mujica">José Alberto "Pepe" Mujica Cordano</a>, Uruguayan <a href="/wiki/Politician" title="Politician">politician</a>, former <a href="/wiki/Guerrilla_warfare" title="Guerrilla warfare">guerrilla</a> with the <a href="/wiki/Tupamaros" title="Tupamaros">Tupamaros</a>, 40th <a href="/wiki/List_of_Presidents_of_Uruguay" class="mw-redirect" title="List of Presidents of Uruguay">President of Uruguay</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Jos%C3%A9_Celestino_Mutis" title="José Celestino Mutis">José Celestino Bruno Mutis y Bosio</a>, Spanish <a href="/wiki/Priesthood_in_the_Catholic_Church" title="Priesthood in the Catholic Church">Catholic priest</a>, <a href="/wiki/Physician" title="Physician">medical practitioner</a>, <a href="/wiki/Botany" title="Botany">botanist</a>, <a href="/wiki/Mathematician" title="Mathematician">mathematician</a> and <a href="/wiki/Painting" title="Painting">artist</a></li></ul>
</div>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="N">N</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Jos%C3%A9&amp;action=edit&amp;section=23" title="Edit section: N">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<div class="div-col columns column-width" style="-moz-column-width: 22em; -webkit-column-width: 22em; column-width: 22em;">
<ul><li><a href="/wiki/Jos%C3%A9_Luis_Narom" title="José Luis Narom">José Luis Narom</a>, also known as José Luis Morán, German-born Spanish <a href="/wiki/Composer" title="Composer">composer</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Jos%C3%A9_Neto_(basketball)" title="José Neto (basketball)">José Alves dos Santos Neto</a>, Brazilian professional <a href="/wiki/Basketball" title="Basketball">basketball</a> coach</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Jos%C3%A9_Neto_(musician)" title="José Neto (musician)">José Pires de Almeida Neto</a>, Brazilian <a href="/wiki/Jazz" title="Jazz">jazz</a> <a href="/wiki/Guitarist" title="Guitarist">guitarist</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Jos%C3%A9_Sebasti%C3%A3o_de_Almeida_Neto" title="José Sebastião de Almeida Neto">José Sebastião de Almeida Neto</a>, Portuguese <a href="/wiki/Bishop_in_the_Catholic_Church" title="Bishop in the Catholic Church">Catholic bishop</a> and <a href="/wiki/Cardinal_(Catholic_Church)" title="Cardinal (Catholic Church)">cardinal</a> who also served in Africa, joined the <a href="/wiki/Order_of_Friars_Minor" title="Order of Friars Minor">Franciscan friars (O.F.M. Disc.)</a> after ordination taking the religious name Joseph of the Sacred Heart, nominated by <a href="/wiki/Lu%C3%ADs_I_of_Portugal" title="Luís I of Portugal">King Luís I</a> first as Bishop of Angola e Congo (now known as the <a href="/wiki/Roman_Catholic_Archdiocese_of_Luanda" title="Roman Catholic Archdiocese of Luanda">Archdiocese of Luanda</a>), then as <a href="/wiki/Patriarchate_of_Lisbon" title="Patriarchate of Lisbon">Patriarch of Lisbon</a> using the name Dom José III, made a Cardinal by <a href="/wiki/Pope_Leo_XIII" title="Pope Leo XIII">Pope Leo XIII</a> in 1884</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Bernard_J._Nolker" title="Bernard J. Nolker">Bernard Joseph Nolker</a>, known in Brazil as Bernardo José Nolker, American-born Brazilian <a href="/wiki/Bishop_in_the_Catholic_Church" title="Bishop in the Catholic Church">Catholic bishop</a>, member of the <a href="/wiki/Congregation_of_the_Most_Holy_Redeemer" title="Congregation of the Most Holy Redeemer">Congregation of the Most Holy Redeemer</a> (C.Ss.R), Bishop of <a href="/wiki/Roman_Catholic_Diocese_of_Paranagu%C3%A1" title="Roman Catholic Diocese of Paranaguá">Paranaguá</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Jos%C3%A9_Maur%C3%ADcio_Nunes_Garcia" title="José Maurício Nunes Garcia">José Maurício Nunes Garcia</a>, Brazilian <a href="/wiki/Priesthood_in_the_Catholic_Church" title="Priesthood in the Catholic Church">Catholic priest</a> and <a href="/wiki/Classical_period_(music)" title="Classical period (music)">Classical</a> <a href="/wiki/Composer" title="Composer">composer</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Jos%C3%A9_Neves" title="José Neves">José Neves</a> (born 1974), Portuguese billionaire businessman, founder of Farfetch</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Jos%C3%A9_N%C3%BA%C3%B1ez_(President_of_Nicaragua)" title="José Núñez (President of Nicaragua)">José Núñez</a>, Nicaraguan <a href="/wiki/Politician" title="Politician">politician</a>, several times <a href="/wiki/President_of_Nicaragua" title="President of Nicaragua">Head of State of Nicaragua</a></li></ul>
</div>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="O">O</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Jos%C3%A9&amp;action=edit&amp;section=24" title="Edit section: O">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<div class="div-col columns column-width" style="-moz-column-width: 22em; -webkit-column-width: 22em; column-width: 22em;"> 
<ul><li><a href="/wiki/Ignacio_Montes_de_Oca_y_Obreg%C3%B3n" title="Ignacio Montes de Oca y Obregón">Ignacio Montes de Oca y Obregón</a>, Mexican <a href="/wiki/Bishop_in_the_Catholic_Church" title="Bishop in the Catholic Church">Catholic bishop</a>, Bishop of <a href="/wiki/Roman_Catholic_Diocese_of_Ciudad_Victoria" title="Roman Catholic Diocese of Ciudad Victoria">Ciudad Victoria</a>, then Bishop of San Luis (now known as the <a href="/wiki/Roman_Catholic_Archdiocese_of_San_Luis_Potos%C3%AD" title="Roman Catholic Archdiocese of San Luis Potosí">Archdiocese of San Luis Potosí</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Juan_Jos%C3%A9_Omella" title="Juan José Omella">Juan José Omella i Omella</a>, Spanish <a href="/wiki/Bishop_in_the_Catholic_Church" title="Bishop in the Catholic Church">Catholic bishop</a> and <a href="/wiki/Cardinal_(Catholic_Church)" title="Cardinal (Catholic Church)">cardinal</a>, <a href="/wiki/Auxiliary_Bishop" class="mw-redirect" title="Auxiliary Bishop">Auxiliary Bishop</a> of <a href="/wiki/Roman_Catholic_Archdiocese_of_Zaragoza" title="Roman Catholic Archdiocese of Zaragoza">Zaragoza</a>, Bishop of <a href="/wiki/Roman_Catholic_Diocese_of_Barbastro-Monz%C3%B3n" title="Roman Catholic Diocese of Barbastro-Monzón">Barbastro-Monzón</a>, <a href="/wiki/Apostolic_Administrator" class="mw-redirect" title="Apostolic Administrator">Apostolic Administrator</a> of <a href="/wiki/Roman_Catholic_Diocese_of_Huesca" title="Roman Catholic Diocese of Huesca">Huesca</a> and of <a href="/wiki/Roman_Catholic_Diocese_of_Jaca" title="Roman Catholic Diocese of Jaca">Jaca</a>, Bishop of <a href="/wiki/Roman_Catholic_Diocese_of_Calahorra_y_La_Calzada-Logro%C3%B1o" title="Roman Catholic Diocese of Calahorra y La Calzada-Logroño">Calahorra y La Calzada-Logroño</a>, and <a href="/wiki/Archbishop" title="Archbishop">Archbishop</a> of <a href="/wiki/Roman_Catholic_Archdiocese_of_Barcelona" title="Roman Catholic Archdiocese of Barcelona">Barcelona</a>, made Cardinal by <a href="/wiki/Pope_Francis" title="Pope Francis">Pope Francis</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Jos%C3%A9_Clemente_Orozco" title="José Clemente Orozco">José Clemente Orozco</a>, Mexican <a href="/wiki/Modern_art" title="Modern art">early modern artist</a> especially known as a <a href="/wiki/Genre_painter" class="mw-redirect" title="Genre painter">genre painter</a>, <a href="/wiki/Mural" title="Mural">muralist</a> and <a href="/wiki/Lithography" title="Lithography">lithographer</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Francisco_Orozco_y_Jim%C3%A9nez" title="Francisco Orozco y Jiménez">José Francisco Orozco y Jiménez</a>, Mexican <a href="/wiki/Bishop_in_the_Catholic_Church" title="Bishop in the Catholic Church">Catholic bishop</a>,  Bishop of <a href="/wiki/Chiapas" title="Chiapas">Chiapas</a>, then <a href="/wiki/Archbishop" title="Archbishop">Archbishop</a> of <a href="/wiki/Guadalajara" title="Guadalajara">Guadalajara</a></li>

<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="P">P</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Jos%C3%A9&amp;action=edit&amp;section=25" title="Edit section: P">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>

<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Q">Q</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Jos%C3%A9&amp;action=edit&amp;section=26" title="Edit section: Q">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>

<ul><li><a href="/wiki/Jos%C3%A9_Humberto_Quintero_Parra" title="José Humberto Quintero Parra">José Humberto Quintero Parra</a>, Venezuelan <a href="/wiki/Bishop_in_the_Catholic_Church" title="Bishop in the Catholic Church">Catholic bishop</a> and <a href="/wiki/Cardinal_(Catholic_Church)" title="Cardinal (Catholic Church)">cardinal</a>, <a href="/wiki/Coadjutor_bishop" title="Coadjutor bishop">Coadjutor Archbishop</a> then <a href="/wiki/Archbishop" title="Archbishop">Archbishop</a> of <a href="/wiki/Roman_Catholic_Archdiocese_of_M%C3%A9rida_in_Venezuela" title="Roman Catholic Archdiocese of Mérida in Venezuela">Mérida</a>, made Cardinal by <a href="/wiki/Pope_John_XXIII" title="Pope John XXIII">Pope John XXIII</a> in 1961, the first Venezuelan so appointed</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Jos%C3%A9_Quiroga" title="José Quiroga">José Quiroga</a>, Chilean-born <a href="/wiki/Cardiology" title="Cardiology">cardiologist</a> now based in America, co-founder and medical director of the <a href="/wiki/Program_for_Torture_Victims" title="Program for Torture Victims">Program for Torture Victims</a>, Vice-President of the <a href="/wiki/International_Rehabilitation_Council_for_Torture_Victims" title="International Rehabilitation Council for Torture Victims">International Rehabilitation Council for Torture Victims</a></li></ul>
</div>

<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="S">S</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Jos%C3%A9&amp;action=edit&amp;section=28" title="Edit section: S">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<div class="div-col columns column-width" style="-moz-column-width: 22em; -webkit-column-width: 22em; column-width: 22em;"> 
<ul><li><a href="/wiki/Jos%C3%A9_Sabogal" title="José Sabogal">José Sabogal</a>, Peruvian early modern <a href="/wiki/Painting" title="Painting">painter</a> and <a href="/wiki/Mural" title="Mural">muralist</a>, recognised as a leader in revival of <a href="/wiki/Indigenism" title="Indigenism">indigeniststyle</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Jos%C3%A9_de_Jes%C3%BAs_Sahag%C3%BAn_de_la_Parra" title="José de Jesús Sahagún de la Parra">José de Jesús Sahagún de la Parra</a>, Mexican <a href="/wiki/Bishop_in_the_Catholic_Church" title="Bishop in the Catholic Church">Catholic bishop</a>, Bishop of <a href="/wiki/Roman_Catholic_Diocese_of_Tula" title="Roman Catholic Diocese of Tula">Tula</a>, then Bishop of <a href="/wiki/Roman_Catholic_Diocese_of_Ciudad_L%C3%A1zaro_C%C3%A1rdenas" title="Roman Catholic Diocese of Ciudad Lázaro Cárdenas">Cuidad Lázaro Cárdenas</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Jos%C3%A9_Hip%C3%B3lito_Salas" title="José Hipólito Salas"> José Hipólito Salas y Toro</a>, Chilean Catholic <a href="/wiki/Theologian" class="mw-redirect" title="Theologian">theologian</a> and <a href="/wiki/Bishop_in_the_Catholic_Church" title="Bishop in the Catholic Church">bishop</a>, Bishop of Concepción (now known as the <a href="/wiki/Roman_Catholic_Archdiocese_of_Concepci%C3%B3n" title="Roman Catholic Archdiocese of Concepción">Concepción</a>, offered a <a href="/wiki/Cardinal_(Catholic_Church)" title="Cardinal (Catholic Church)">cardinalate</a> by <a href="/wiki/Pope_Pius_IX" title="Pope Pius IX">Pope Pius IX</a> which he refused</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Jos%C3%A9_Mariano_Salas" title="José Mariano Salas">José Mariano Salas</a>, Mexican <a href="/wiki/General_officer" title="General officer">general</a>, twice <a href="/wiki/List_of_heads_of_state_of_Mexico" title="List of heads of state of Mexico">Interim President of Mexico</a>, <a href="/wiki/Regent" title="Regent">Co-Regent</a> of Mexico under the <a href="/wiki/Second_Mexican_Empire" title="Second Mexican Empire">Second Mexican Empire</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Jos%C3%A9_Salazar_L%C3%B3pez" title="José Salazar López">José Salazar López</a>, Mexican <a href="/wiki/Bishop_in_the_Catholic_Church" title="Bishop in the Catholic Church">Catholic bishop</a> and <a href="/wiki/Cardinal_(Catholic_Church)" title="Cardinal (Catholic Church)">cardinal</a>, <a href="/wiki/Coadjutor_bishop" title="Coadjutor bishop">Coadjutor Bishop</a>, Bishop of <a href="/wiki/Roman_Catholic_Diocese_of_Zamora_in_Mexico" title="Roman Catholic Diocese of Zamora in Mexico">Zamora</a>, then <a href="/wiki/Archbishop" title="Archbishop">Archbishop</a> of <a href="/wiki/Roman_Catholic_Archdiocese_of_Guadalajara" title="Roman Catholic Archdiocese of Guadalajara">Guadalajara</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Jos%C3%A9_Antonio_Salcedo" title="José Antonio Salcedo">José Antonio Salcedo y Ramírez</a>, known as <i>Pepillo</i>, Spanish-born to parents from Santo Domingo, led the <a href="/wiki/Dominican_Restoration_War" title="Dominican Restoration War">civil war</a> for restoration of the Dominican Republic, became 1st <a href="/wiki/List_of_Presidents_of_the_Dominican_Republic" class="mw-redirect" title="List of Presidents of the Dominican Republic">head of state</a> after the Spanish withdrawal, later opposed and assassinated by Nationalists allegedly for his support for Spain</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Jos%C3%A9_Salvatierra" title="José Salvatierra">José Andres Salvatierra López</a>, Costa Rican international <a href="/wiki/Association_football" title="Association football">football</a> player</li>

<li><a href="/wiki/Jose_Tomas_Sanchez" title="Jose Tomas Sanchez">Jose Tomas Sanchez</a>, Filipino <a href="/wiki/Bishop_in_the_Catholic_Church" title="Bishop in the Catholic Church">Catholic bishop</a> and <a href="/wiki/Cardinal_(Catholic_Church)" title="Cardinal (Catholic Church)">cardinal</a>, <a href="/wiki/Auxiliary_bishop" title="Auxiliary bishop">Auxiliary Bishop</a> of <a href="/wiki/Roman_Catholic_Archdiocese_of_C%C3%A1ceres" title="Roman Catholic Archdiocese of Cáceres">Cáceres</a>, <a href="/wiki/Coadjutor_bishop" title="Coadjutor bishop">Coadjutor Bishop</a> then Bishop of <a href="/wiki/Roman_Catholic_Diocese_of_Lucena" title="Roman Catholic Diocese of Lucena">Lucena</a>, Archbishop of <a href="/wiki/Roman_Catholic_Archdiocese_of_Nueva_Segovia" title="Roman Catholic Archdiocese of Nueva Segovia">Nueva Segovia</a>, appointment to the <a href="/wiki/Roman_Curia" title="Roman Curia">Roman Curia</a>, first to the <a href="/wiki/Congregation_for_the_Evangelization_of_Peoples" title="Congregation for the Evangelization of Peoples">Congregation for the Evangelization of Peoples</a> then simultaneously to the <a href="/wiki/Congregation_for_the_Clergy" title="Congregation for the Clergy">Congregation for the Clergy</a> and the <a href="/wiki/Administration_of_the_Patrimony_of_the_Apostolic_See" title="Administration of the Patrimony of the Apostolic See">Administration of the Patrimony of the Apostolic See</a>, made Cardinal Deacon by <a href="/wiki/Pope_John_Paul_II" title="Pope John Paul II">Pope John Paul II</a> in 1991 and elevated to Cardinal Priest by the same pope in 2002</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Jos%C3%A9_S%C3%A1nchez-Guerra_y_Mart%C3%ADnez" title="José Sánchez-Guerra y Martínez">José Sánchez-Guerra y Martínez</a>, Spanish <a href="/wiki/Journalist" title="Journalist">journalist</a>, <a href="/wiki/Lawyer" title="Lawyer">lawyer</a> and <a href="/wiki/Politician" title="Politician">politician</a>, <a href="/wiki/List_of_Prime_Ministers_of_Spain" class="mw-redirect" title="List of Prime Ministers of Spain">Prime Minister</a> under <a href="/wiki/Alfonso_XIII_of_Spain" title="Alfonso XIII of Spain">King Alfonso XIII</a></li>

<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="U">U</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Jos%C3%A9&amp;action=edit&amp;section=30" title="Edit section: U">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<div class="div-col columns column-width" style="-moz-column-width: 22em; -webkit-column-width: 22em; column-width: 22em;">
<ul><li><a href="/wiki/Jos%C3%A9_Domingo_Ulloa_Mendieta" title="José Domingo Ulloa Mendieta">José Domingo Ulloa Mendieta</a>, Panamanian <a href="/wiki/Friar" title="Friar">friar</a> of the <a href="/wiki/Order_of_Saint_Augustine" title="Order of Saint Augustine">Order of Saint Augustine</a> (O.S.A.) and <a href="/wiki/Bishop_in_the_Catholic_Church" title="Bishop in the Catholic Church">Catholic bishop</a>, <a href="/wiki/Auxiliary_bishop" title="Auxiliary bishop">Auxiliary Bishop</a> then <a href="/wiki/Archbishop" title="Archbishop">Archbishop</a> of <a href="/wiki/Roman_Catholic_Archdiocese_of_Panam%C3%A1" title="Roman Catholic Archdiocese of Panamá">Panamá</a>, opponent to <a href="/wiki/Capital_punishment" title="Capital punishment">capital punishment</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Jos%C3%A9_Ure%C3%B1a" title="José Ureña">José Miguel Ureña Rodriguez</a>, Dominican professional <a href="/wiki/Basketball" title="Basketball">basketball</a> player</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Jos%C3%A9_Evaristo_Uriburu" title="José Evaristo Uriburu">José Félix Evaristo de Uriburu y Álvarez de Arenales</a>, Argentine <a href="/wiki/Diplomat" title="Diplomat">diplomat</a> and <a href="/wiki/Politician" title="Politician">politician</a>, 8th <a href="/wiki/List_of_Vice_Presidents_of_Argentina" class="mw-redirect" title="List of Vice Presidents of Argentina">Vice President of Argentina</a>, 1st de facto <a href="/wiki/List_of_heads_of_state_of_Argentina" title="List of heads of state of Argentina">President of Argentina</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Jos%C3%A9_Mar%C3%ADa_de_Urquinaona_y_Vidot" title="José María de Urquinaona y Vidot">José María Urquinaona y Bidot</a> (or Vidot), Spanish <a href="/wiki/Bishop_in_the_Catholic_Church" title="Bishop in the Catholic Church">Catholic bishop</a>, Bishop of Barcelona (now known as the <a href="/wiki/Roman_Catholic_Archdiocese_of_Barcelona" title="Roman Catholic Archdiocese of Barcelona">Archdiocese of Barcelona</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Jos%C3%A9_Mar%C3%ADa_Usandizaga" title="José María Usandizaga">José María Usandizaga</a>, Spanish <a href="/wiki/Basque_people" class="mw-redirect" title="Basque people">Basque</a> <a href="/wiki/Composer" title="Composer">composer</a></li></ul>
</div>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="V">V</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Jos%C3%A9&amp;action=edit&amp;section=31" title="Edit section: V">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<div class="div-col columns column-width" style="-moz-column-width: 22em; -webkit-column-width: 22em; column-width: 22em;">
<ul><li><a href="/wiki/Jos%C3%A9_Bordas_Valdez" title="José Bordas Valdez">José Bordas Valdez</a>, Dominican <a href="/wiki/Politician" title="Politician">politician</a>, 2nd Provisional <a href="/wiki/List_of_Presidents_of_the_Dominican_Republic" class="mw-redirect" title="List of Presidents of the Dominican Republic">President</a> appointed by the <a href="/wiki/Congress_of_the_Dominican_Republic" title="Congress of the Dominican Republic">Congress of the Dominican Republic</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Jos%C3%A9_Valent%C3%ADn" title="José Valentín">José Valentín</a>, Puerto Rican <a href="/wiki/Baseball" title="Baseball">baseball</a> player</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Jos%C3%A9_Gregorio_Valera" title="José Gregorio Valera">José Gregorio Valera</a>, Venezuelan <a href="/wiki/Revolution" title="Revolution">revolutionary</a> and <a href="/wiki/Politician" title="Politician">politician</a>, <a href="/wiki/List_of_Presidents_of_Venezuela" class="mw-redirect" title="List of Presidents of Venezuela">President of Venezuela</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Jos%C3%A9_S%C3%B3tero_Valero_Ruz" title="José Sótero Valero Ruz">José Sótero Valero Ruz</a>, Venezuelan <a href="/wiki/Bishop_in_the_Catholic_Church" title="Bishop in the Catholic Church">Catholic bishop</a>, Bishop of <a href="/wiki/Roman_Catholic_Diocese_of_Guanare" title="Roman Catholic Diocese of Guanare">Guanare</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Jos%C3%A9_Cecilio_del_Valle" title="José Cecilio del Valle">José Cecilio Díaz Del Valle</a>, nicknamed <i>el sabio</i> (The Wise), Guatemalan-born Mexican <a href="/wiki/Philosopher" title="Philosopher">philosopher</a>, <a href="/wiki/Politician" title="Politician">politician</a>, <a href="/wiki/Lawyer" title="Lawyer">lawyer</a>, and <a href="/wiki/Journalist" title="Journalist">journalist</a>, author of the <a href="/wiki/Act_of_Independence_of_Central_America" title="Act of Independence of Central America">Act of Independence of Central America</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Jos%C3%A9_Desiderio_Valverde" title="José Desiderio Valverde">José Desiderio Valverde Pérez</a>, Spanish soldier to the rank of <a href="/wiki/General_officer" title="General officer">general</a>, served with distinction in the Spanish colonies including appointment as 4th and last <a href="/wiki/List_of_Presidents_of_the_Dominican_Republic" class="mw-redirect" title="List of Presidents of the Dominican Republic">Captain General of Santo Domingo</a> during the <a href="/wiki/Spanish_occupation_of_the_Dominican_Republic" title="Spanish occupation of the Dominican Republic">Spanish occupation</a>, after Spanish withdrawal appointed as governor-general of the <a href="/wiki/Philippine_islands" class="mw-redirect" title="Philippine islands">Philippine islands</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Jos%C3%A9_Valverde" title="José Valverde">José Rafael Valverde</a>, Dominican-born American <a href="/wiki/Baseball" title="Baseball">baseball</a> player</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Jose_Antonio_Vargas" title="Jose Antonio Vargas">Jose Antonio Vargas</a>, Filipino American <a href="/wiki/Journalist" title="Journalist">journalist</a> and <a href="/wiki/Pulitzer_Prize" title="Pulitzer Prize">Pulitzer Prize</a> winner</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Jos%C3%A9_Mar%C3%ADa_Vargas" title="José María Vargas">José María Vargas Ponce</a>, Venezuelan <a href="/wiki/Physician" title="Physician">medical practitioner</a>, <a href="/wiki/Revolution" title="Revolution">revolutionary</a> and <a href="/wiki/Politician" title="Politician">politician</a>, <a href="/wiki/List_of_Presidents_of_Venezuela" class="mw-redirect" title="List of Presidents of Venezuela">President of Venezuela</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Jos%C3%A9_Vasconcelos" title="José Vasconcelos">José Vasconcelos Calderón</a>, Mexican <a href="/wiki/Writer" title="Writer">writer</a>, <a href="/wiki/Philosopher" title="Philosopher">philosopher</a> and <a href="/wiki/Politician" title="Politician">politician</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Jos%C3%A9_Leite_de_Vasconcelos" title="José Leite de Vasconcelos">José Leite de Vasconcelos</a>, Portuguese <a href="/wiki/Ethnography" title="Ethnography">ethnographer</a> and <a href="/wiki/Philology" title="Philology">philologist</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Jos%C3%A9_Mauro_de_Vasconcelos" title="José Mauro de Vasconcelos">José Mauro de Vasconcelos</a>, Brazilian <a href="/wiki/Writer" title="Writer">writer</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Jos%C3%A9_Antonio_V%C3%A9lez" title="José Antonio Vélez">José Antonio Vélez Jiménez</a>, known as <i>Ñoño</i> (Ninth), Spanish professional <a href="/wiki/Association_football" title="Association football">football</a> player</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Jos%C3%A9_Augusto_Ferreira_Veiga" title="José Augusto Ferreira Veiga">José Augusto Ferreira Veiga</a>, Viscount of Arneiro, born in <a href="/wiki/Portuguese_Macau" title="Portuguese Macau">Portuguese Macau</a>, Portuguese <a href="/wiki/Composer" title="Composer">composer</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Jos%C3%A9_Miguel_de_Velasco_Franco" title="José Miguel de Velasco Franco">José Miguel de Velasco Franco</a>, Vice-President then four times <a href="/wiki/President_of_Bolivia" title="President of Bolivia">President of Bolivia</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Jos%C3%A9_Mar%C3%ADa_Velasco_G%C3%B3mez" title="José María Velasco Gómez">José María Tranquilino Francisco de Jesús Velasco Gómez Obregón</a>, generally known as José María Velasco, Mexican <a href="/wiki/Painting" title="Painting">painter</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Jos%C3%A9_Nieto_Vel%C3%A1zquez" title="José Nieto Velázquez">José Nieto Velázquez</a>, Spanish <a href="/wiki/Court_(royal)" class="mw-redirect" title="Court (royal)">court official</a>, <a href="/wiki/Chamberlain_(office)" title="Chamberlain (office)">chamberlain</a> to <a href="/wiki/Elisabeth_Farnese" title="Elisabeth Farnese">Queen Elisabeth of Spain</a>, keeper of the royal <a href="/wiki/Tapestry" title="Tapestry">tapestries</a>, possible figure in paintings <a href="/wiki/Portrait_of_a_Man_(Vel%C3%A1zquez)" title="Portrait of a Man (Velázquez)">Portrait of a Man</a> and <i><a href="/wiki/Las_Meninas" title="Las Meninas">Las Meninas</a></i>  by his brother <a href="/wiki/Diego_Vel%C3%A1zquez" title="Diego Velázquez">Diego Velázquez</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Jos%C3%A9_V%C3%A9lez" title="José Vélez">José Velázquez Jiménez</a>, known to the public as José Velez, Spanish <a href="/wiki/Singing" title="Singing">singer</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Jos%C3%A9_Ra%C3%BAl_Vera_L%C3%B3pez" title="José Raúl Vera López">José Raúl Vera López</a>, Mexican <a href="/wiki/Friar" title="Friar">friar</a> of the <a href="/wiki/Dominican_Order" title="Dominican Order">Dominican Order</a> and <a href="/wiki/Bishop_in_the_Catholic_Church" title="Bishop in the Catholic Church">Catholic bishop</a>, Bishop of <a href="/wiki/Roman_Catholic_Diocese_of_Ciudad_Altamirano" title="Roman Catholic Diocese of Ciudad Altamirano">Ciudad Altamirano</a>, <a href="/wiki/Coadjutor_bishop" title="Coadjutor bishop">Coadjutor Bishop</a> of <a href="/wiki/Roman_Catholic_Diocese_of_San_Crist%C3%B3bal_de_Las_Casas" title="Roman Catholic Diocese of San Cristóbal de Las Casas">San Cristóbal de Las Casas</a>, then Bishop of <a href="/wiki/Roman_Catholic_Diocese_of_Saltillo" title="Roman Catholic Diocese of Saltillo">Saltillo</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Jos%C3%A9_Mar%C3%ADa_Verdugo" title="José María Verdugo">José María Verdugo</a>, born in <a href="/wiki/New_Spain" title="New Spain">New Spain</a>, soldier from the <a href="/wiki/Presidio_of_San_Diego" title="Presidio of San Diego">Presidio of San Diego</a>, granted extensive land in present-day <a href="/wiki/California" title="California">California</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Jos%C3%A9_Carlos_Amaral_Vieira" title="José Carlos Amaral Vieira">José Carlos Amaral Vieira</a>, Brazilian <a href="/wiki/Composer" title="Composer">composer</a>, <a href="/wiki/Pianist" title="Pianist">pianist</a>, and <a href="/wiki/Musicology" title="Musicology">musicologist</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Jos%C3%A9_Luis_de_Vilallonga" class="mw-redirect" title="José Luis de Vilallonga">José Luis de Vilallonga</a>, Spanish <a href="/wiki/Nobility" title="Nobility">noble</a> titled Marquis of Castellbell, <a href="/wiki/Author" title="Author">author</a> and <a href="/wiki/Actor" title="Actor">actor</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Jos%C3%A9_Vizca%C3%ADno" title="José Vizcaíno">José Vizcaíno</a>, American <a href="/wiki/Baseball" title="Baseball">baseball</a> player</li></ul>
</div>

<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Z">Z</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Jos%C3%A9&amp;action=edit&amp;section=35" title="Edit section: Z">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<div class="div-col columns column-width" style="-moz-column-width: 22em; -webkit-column-width: 22em; column-width: 22em;">
<ul><li><a href="/wiki/Jos%C3%A9_Luis_Rodr%C3%ADguez_Zapatero" title="José Luis Rodríguez Zapatero">José Luis Rodríguez Zapatero</a>, Spanish <a href="/wiki/Politician" title="Politician">politician</a>, served for two terms as <a href="/wiki/List_of_Prime_Ministers_of_Spain" class="mw-redirect" title="List of Prime Ministers of Spain">Prime Minister</a> under <a href="/wiki/Juan_Carlos_I_of_Spain" title="Juan Carlos I of Spain">King Juan Carlos I</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Jos%C3%A9_Santos_Zelaya" title="José Santos Zelaya">José Santos Zelaya López</a>, Nicaraguan <a href="/wiki/Politician" title="Politician">politician</a>, 11th <a href="/wiki/President_of_Nicaragua" title="President of Nicaragua">President of Nicaragua</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Jose_Zepeda" title="Jose Zepeda">Jose Zepeda</a>, American professional <a href="/wiki/Boxing" title="Boxing">boxer</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Jos%C3%A9_Zorrilla" title="José Zorrilla">José Zorrilla y Moral</a>, Spanish Catholic <a href="/wiki/Romantic_poetry" title="Romantic poetry">Romantic</a> <a href="/wiki/Poet" title="Poet">poet</a> and <a href="/wiki/Playwright" title="Playwright">dramatist</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Jos%C3%A9_Antonio_Laureano_de_Zubir%C3%ADa" title="José Antonio Laureano de Zubiría">José Antonio Laureano de Zubiría y Escalante</a>, Mexican <a href="/wiki/Bishop_in_the_Catholic_Church" title="Bishop in the Catholic Church">Catholic bishop</a>, Bishop of Durango (now known as the <a href="/wiki/Roman_Catholic_Archdiocese_of_Durango" title="Roman Catholic Archdiocese of Durango">Archdiocese of Durango</a>), supporter of the <a href="/wiki/Centralist_Republic_of_Mexico" title="Centralist Republic of Mexico">Centralist Republic of Mexico</a> and critic of the United States' control of the northern part of his diocese</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Jos%C3%A9_Z%C3%BA%C3%B1iga" title="José Zúñiga">José Zúñiga</a>, Honduran-born American screen and television <a href="/wiki/Actor" title="Actor">actor</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Jos%C3%A9_Z%C3%BA%C3%B1iga_(artist)" title="José Zúñiga (artist)">José Zúñiga</a>, Mexican <a href="/wiki/Figurative_art" title="Figurative art">Neo-figurative</a> painter, represented internationally in private and public collections</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Jos%C3%A9_de_Z%C3%BA%C3%B1iga" class="mw-redirect" title="José de Zúñiga">José de Zúñiga</a>, Mexican-born soldier to the ran of <a href="/wiki/Lieutenant_colonel" title="Lieutenant colonel">lieutenant colonel</a>, <a href="/wiki/Settler" title="Settler">settler</a> in <a href="/wiki/California" title="California">California</a> and <a href="/wiki/Arizona" title="Arizona">Arizona</a>, <a href="/wiki/List_of_pre-statehood_mayors_of_San_Diego" title="List of pre-statehood mayors of San Diego">Commandant</a> of the <a href="/wiki/Presidio_of_San_Diego" title="Presidio of San Diego">Presidio of San Diego</a>, member of the <a href="/wiki/Third_Order_of_Saint_Francis" title="Third Order of Saint Francis">Third Order</a> of <a href="/wiki/Franciscans" title="Franciscans">Franciscans</a></li></ul>
</div>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Middle_name">Middle name</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Jos%C3%A9&amp;action=edit&amp;section=36" title="Edit section: Middle name">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<div class="div-col columns column-width" style="-moz-column-width: 22em; -webkit-column-width: 22em; column-width: 22em;">
<ul><li><a href="/wiki/Agostinho_Jos%C3%A9_Sartori" title="Agostinho José Sartori">Agostinho José Sartori</a>, Brazilian <a href="/wiki/Bishop_in_the_Catholic_Church" title="Bishop in the Catholic Church">Catholic bishop</a>, Bishop of <a href="/wiki/Roman_Catholic_Diocese_of_Palmas%E2%80%93Francisco_Beltr%C3%A3o" title="Roman Catholic Diocese of Palmas–Francisco Beltrão">Palmas–Francisco Beltrão</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Airton_Jos%C3%A9_dos_Santos" title="Airton José dos Santos">Airton José dos Santos</a>, Brazilian <a href="/wiki/Bishop_in_the_Catholic_Church" title="Bishop in the Catholic Church">Catholic bishop</a>, Bishop of <a href="/wiki/Roman_Catholic_Diocese_of_Mogi_das_Cruzes" title="Roman Catholic Diocese of Mogi das Cruzes">Mogi das Cruzes</a> and then Archbishop of <a href="/wiki/Roman_Catholic_Archdiocese_of_Campinas" title="Roman Catholic Archdiocese of Campinas">Campinas</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Aloysio_Jos%C3%A9_Leal_Penna" title="Aloysio José Leal Penna">Aloysio José Leal Penna</a>, Brazilian <a href="/wiki/Bishop_in_the_Catholic_Church" title="Bishop in the Catholic Church">Catholic bishop</a>, first as Bishop of <a href="/wiki/Roman_Catholic_Diocese_of_Paulo_Afonso" title="Roman Catholic Diocese of Paulo Afonso">Paulo Afonso</a>, then as Archbishop of <a href="/wiki/Roman_Catholic_Archdiocese_of_Botucatu" title="Roman Catholic Archdiocese of Botucatu">Botucatu</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/%C3%81ngel_Jos%C3%A9_Mac%C3%ADn" title="Ángel José Macín">Ángel José Macín</a>, Argentinian <a href="/wiki/Bishop_in_the_Catholic_Church" title="Bishop in the Catholic Church">Catholic bishop</a>, Bishop of <a href="/wiki/Roman_Catholic_Diocese_of_Reconquista" title="Roman Catholic Diocese of Reconquista">Reconquista</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Ant%C3%B3nio_Jos%C3%A9_de_Almeida" title="António José de Almeida">António José de Almeida</a>, 6th <a href="/wiki/List_of_Presidents_of_Portugal" class="mw-redirect" title="List of Presidents of Portugal">President of Portugal</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Ant%C3%B3nio_Jos%C3%A9_de_%C3%81vila,_1st_Duke_of_%C3%81vila_and_Bolama" title="António José de Ávila, 1st Duke of Ávila and Bolama">António José de Ávila, 1st Duke of Ávila and Bolama</a>, Portuguese <a href="/wiki/Politician" title="Politician">politician</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Antonio_Jos%C3%A9_Cavanilles" title="Antonio José Cavanilles">Antonio José Cavanilles</a>, Spanish <a href="/wiki/Taxonomy_(biology)" title="Taxonomy (biology)">taxonomist</a> and <a href="/wiki/Botany" title="Botany">botanist</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Antonio_Jos%C3%A9_de_Irisarri" title="Antonio José de Irisarri">Antonio José de Irisarri Alonso</a>, Guatemalan <a href="/wiki/Politician" title="Politician">statesman</a>, <a href="/wiki/Journalist" title="Journalist">journalist</a>, and <a href="/wiki/Politician" title="Politician">politician</a>, served as Interim <a href="/wiki/Supreme_Director_of_Chile" title="Supreme Director of Chile">Supreme Director of Chile</a>, considered as one of the fathers of Chilean journalism</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Antonio_Jos%C3%A9" title="Antonio José">Antonio José Martínez Palacios</a>, known as Antonio José, Spanish <a href="/wiki/Composer" title="Composer">composer</a></li>

<li><a href="/wiki/Ram%C3%B3n_Jos%C3%A9_de_Arce" title="Ramón José de Arce"> Ramón José de Arce y Rebollar</a>, Spanish <a href="/wiki/Bishop_in_the_Catholic_Church" title="Bishop in the Catholic Church">Catholic bishop</a>, <a href="/wiki/Archbishop" title="Archbishop">Archbishop</a> of <a href="/wiki/Roman_Catholic_Archdiocese_of_Burgos" title="Roman Catholic Archdiocese of Burgos">Burgos</a>, <a href="/wiki/Grand_Inquisitor" title="Grand Inquisitor">Grand Inquisitor</a> of the <a href="/wiki/Spanish_Inquisition" title="Spanish Inquisition">Spanish Inquisition</a>, Archbishop of <a href="/wiki/Roman_Catholic_Archdiocese_of_Zaragoza" title="Roman Catholic Archdiocese of Zaragoza">Zaragoza</a>, <a href="/wiki/Patriarch_of_the_West_Indies" class="mw-redirect" title="Patriarch of the West Indies">Patriarch of the West Indies</a>, was understood as being pro-French when Spain was <a href="/wiki/Kingdom_of_Spain_(Napoleonic)" class="mw-redirect" title="Kingdom of Spain (Napoleonic)">invaded by the First French Empire</a> and exiled to <a href="/wiki/Paris" title="Paris">Paris</a> when Spain gained independence during the <a href="/wiki/Peninsular_War" title="Peninsular War">Peninsular War</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Rem%C3%ADdio_Jos%C3%A9_Bohn" title="Remídio José Bohn">Remídio José Bohn</a>, Brazilian <a href="/wiki/Bishop_in_the_Catholic_Church" title="Bishop in the Catholic Church">Catholic bishop</a>, <a href="/wiki/Auxiliary_bishop" title="Auxiliary bishop">Auxiliary Bishop</a> of <a href="/wiki/Roman_Catholic_Archdiocese_of_Porto_Alegre" title="Roman Catholic Archdiocese of Porto Alegre">Porto Alegre</a>, then Bishop of <a href="/wiki/Roman_Catholic_Diocese_of_Cachoeira_do_Sul" title="Roman Catholic Diocese of Cachoeira do Sul">Cachoeira do Sul</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Ricardo_Jos%C3%A9_Weberberger" title="Ricardo José Weberberger">Ricardo José Weberberger</a>, Austrian-born Brazilian <a href="/wiki/Order_of_Saint_Benedict" class="mw-redirect" title="Order of Saint Benedict">Benedictine monk</a> (O.S.B.) and <a href="/wiki/Bishop_in_the_Catholic_Church" title="Bishop in the Catholic Church">Catholic bishop</a>, Bishop of <a href="/wiki/Roman_Catholic_Diocese_of_Barreiras" title="Roman Catholic Diocese of Barreiras">Barreiras</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Urbano_Jos%C3%A9_Allgayer" title="Urbano José Allgayer">Urbano José Allgayer</a>, Brazilian <a href="/wiki/Bishop_in_the_Catholic_Church" title="Bishop in the Catholic Church">Catholic bishop</a>, <a href="/wiki/Auxiliary_bishop" title="Auxiliary bishop">Auxiliary Bishop</a> of <a href="/wiki/Roman_Catholic_Archdiocese_of_Porto_Alegre" title="Roman Catholic Archdiocese of Porto Alegre">Porto Alegre</a>, then Bishop of Passo Fundo (now known as the <a href="/wiki/Roman_Catholic_Archdiocese_of_Passo_Fundo" title="Roman Catholic Archdiocese of Passo Fundo">Archdiocese of Passo Fundo</a></li></ul>
</div>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Surname">Surname</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Jos%C3%A9&amp;action=edit&amp;section=37" title="Edit section: Surname">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<ul><li><a href="/w/index.php?title=Ajai_Jose&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="Ajai Jose (page does not exist)">Ajai Jose</a>, Indian screen <a href="/wiki/Actor" title="Actor">actor</a></li>
<li><a href="/w/index.php?title=Ajay_Jose&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="Ajay Jose (page does not exist)">Ajay Jose</a>, Indian <a href="/wiki/Malayalam_cinema" title="Malayalam cinema">Malayalam</a> <a href="/wiki/Film_producer" title="Film producer">film producer</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Edward_Jos%C3%A9" title="Edward José">Edward José</a>, Belgian film director and <a href="/wiki/Actor" title="Actor">actor</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/F._Sionil_Jos%C3%A9" title="F. Sionil José">Francisco Sionil José</a>, Filipino <a href="/wiki/Novelist" title="Novelist">novelist</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Jorge_V._Jos%C3%A9" title="Jorge V. José">Jorge V. José</a>, Mexican <a href="/wiki/Physicist" title="Physicist">physicist</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Mohan_Jose" title="Mohan Jose">Mohan Jose</a>, Indian <a href="/wiki/Actor" title="Actor">actor</a> in <a href="/wiki/Malayalam_cinema" title="Malayalam cinema">Malayalam films</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Nicholas_Jose" title="Nicholas Jose">Nicholas Jose</a>, British-born Australian <a href="/wiki/Novelist" title="Novelist">novelist</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Richard_Jose" title="Richard Jose">Richard Jose</a>, British-born American <a href="/wiki/Singing" title="Singing">singer</a></li></ul>
